SAMPLE      Natural elements Ti,V,Cr,Fe,Cu,Ga,Zr,Mo,W,Pt          20416  1   83 
            and Pb.                                               20416  1   84 
            Monoisotopic natural elements Sc,Co,Y,Nb,Rh,Tm,       20416  1   85 
            Au, and Bi, (and Lu and Ta).                          20416  1   86 
            Separated isotopes for the even isotopes of Se,Nd,    20416  1   87 
            Sm,Eu-151, and the main isotopes of Gd,W,Tl and       20416  1   88 
            Pb, and For U-238.                                    20416  1   89 
            Lu-175 and Ta-181 are only the major components of    20416  1   90 
            the natural elements.                                 20416  1   91 
            Calculation by S.Pearlstein, Nuclear Data B,          20416  1   92 
            Section A, 3(1967) used for correcting Se-74 and      20416  1   93 
            Se-77 contributions and to derive (n,2n) cross-       20416  1   94 
            sections of Fe-56 and Lu-175.                         20416  1   95 
            About 15 gram. disks of 25 mm diam. Metallic          20416  1   96 
            samples except for separated isotopes of Se, Sm,      20416  1   97 
            Nd and Gd, which were oxides.                         20416  1   98

ASSUMED    (ASSUM,98-CF-252(0,F),PR,NU)                           20416  1  129 
ANALYSIS    Determination of the neutron multiplicity             20416  1  130 
            distribution for the detected events.                 20416  1  131 
CORRECTION  Background correction.                                20416  1  132 
            For dead time losses.                                 20416  1  133 
            Efficiency correction for difference of Cf252 fission 20416  1  134 
            neutron and (n,2n) neutron spectra.                   20416  1  135 
            Multiple event correction.                            20416  1  136 
            For events not induced in sample.                     20416  1  137 
            For (n,2n) reactions induced by non-monoenergetic     20416  1  138 
            neutrons.                                             20416  1  139 
            Correction in the flux measurement.                   20416  1  140 
            For the effect of (n,2n) reaction in the axial tube   20416  1  141 
            of scintillator tank - estimated to be negligible.    20416  1  142 
            For reactions induced by degraded neutrons ( -3%)     20416  1  143 
            and loss of secondary neutrons in sample ( +0.5%) .   20416  1  144 
COMMENT     The direct detection technique of emitted neutrons    20416  1  145 
            used in this experiment is not limited to nuclei      20416  1  146 
            with suitable activity characteristics of             20416  1  147 
            residual isotopes as it is the case for activation    20416  1  148 
            measurements.                                         20416  1  149
